TITLE      Measurement of the 159Tb(n, gamma) cross section at    3289900100003 
           the CSNS Back-n facility                               3289900100004 
AUTHOR     (S.Zhang,G.Li,W.Jiang,D.X.Wang,J.Ren,M.Huang,E.T.Li,   3289900100005 
           J.Y.Tang,X.C.Ruan,H.W.Wang,Z.H.Li,Y.S.Chen,L.X.Liu,    3289900100006 
           X.X.Li,Q.W.Fan,R.R.Fan,X.R.Hu,J.C.Wang,X.Li,D.D.Niu,   3289900100007 
           N.Song,M.Gu)                                           3289900100008 
REFERENCE  (J,PR/C,107,045809,2023)                               3289900100009 
           #doi:10.1103/PhysRevC.107.045809                       3289900100010 
INSTITUTE  (3CPRCPR) Inner Mongolia Minzu University, Tongliao    3289900100011 
           (3CPRIHP,3CPRAEP,3CPRSZN)                              3289900100012 
           (3CPRCPR) Shanghai Advanced Research Institute,        3289900100013 
                     Chinese Academy of Sciences, Shanghai        3289900100014 
           (3CPRNRS)                                              3289900100015 
FACILITY   (SYNCH,3CPRIHP) CSNS Back-n facility in China.         3289900100016 
INC-SOURCE (SPALL) Neutrons were produced via the spallation      3289900100017 
           reactions by bombarding a massive tungsten target      3289900100018 
           with a 1.6 GeV proton beam, operating at a 25 Hz       3289900100019 
           repetition rate, and collimated to a 30 mm diameter    3289900100020 
           beam spot at the sample position.                      3289900100021 
METHOD     (TOF,PHWT) The neutron energies ranging from thermal   3289900100022 
           to a few hundred MeV were determined using the time    3289900100023 
           of flight (TOF) method with a 76 m long flight path.   3289900100024 
           Saturated resonance technique with the 197Au 4.9 eV    3289900100025 
           resonance and 159Tb 11.1 eV resonance.                 3289900100026 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) The neutron capture yields were studied using   3289900100027 
           the total energy measurement principle based on an     3289900100028 
           array of four C6D6 detectors with the pulse height     3289900100029 
           weighting techniques (PHWT).                           3289900100030 
           (SILI,FISCH) The neutron flux in the energy range of   3289900100031 
           1 eV to 100 MeV was obtained with a combination of     3289900100032 
           the data from dedicated measurements of the 6LiF-      3289900100033 
           silicon (Li-Si) detector array and the 235U loaded     3289900100034 
           multilayer fission chamber. The Li-Si detector neutron 3289900100035 
           flux was normalized to 235U data at 10-20 keV since    3289900100036 
           its position was about 20 m away from the sample.      3289900100037 
SAMPLE     A metallic terbium sample of natural abundance with a  3289900100038 
           thickness of 0.2 mm was used for the 159Tb(n,g)        3289900100039 
           reaction study. The 197Au sample was used as the       3289900100040 
           standard for calculating the relative cross section    3289900100041 
           of 159Tb(n,g) in neutron energies ranging from 2       3289900100042 
           keV to 1 MeV. The natPb samples were used to           3289900100043 
           normalize the neutron fluence and to evaluate the      3289900100044 
           in-beam gamma-rays and scattered-neutron backgrounds.  3289900100045 
           *******************************************************3289900100046 
                  Thickness  Diameter      Mass   Area density    3289900100047 
           Sample      (mm)      (mm)      (mg)      (atom/b)     3289900100048 
           *******************************************************3289900100049 
           natTb       0.20        30   1169.14       6.27E-4     3289900100050 
           197Au       0.10        30   1357.17       5.87E-4     3289900100051 
           natPb       0.53        30   4249.75       1.75E-3     3289900100052 
           *******************************************************3289900100053 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-S,,5.) The statistical uncertainty is less than   3289900100054 
           1% below 100 eV and less than 5% between 2 keV and     3289900100055 
           1 MeV.                                                 3289900100056 
           (ERR-2) Pulse height weighting functions 3.0%          3289900100057 
           (ERR-3) Background subtraction with filters 8.6%       3289900100058 
           (ERR-4) Normalization factor 1.0%                      3289900100059 
           (ERR-5) Flight path 0.08%                              3289900100060 
           (ERR-6) Sample impurities 0.01%                        3289900100061
